\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00131}00131 \textcolor{comment}{//   Starting with version 1.06, the rasterizer was replaced with a new,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00132}00132 \textcolor{comment}{//   faster and generally-\/more-\/precise rasterizer. The new rasterizer more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00133}00133 \textcolor{comment}{//   accurately measures pixel coverage for anti-\/aliasing, except in the case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00134}00134 \textcolor{comment}{//   where multiple shapes overlap, in which case it overestimates the AA pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00135}00135 \textcolor{comment}{//   coverage. Thus, anti-\/aliasing of intersecting shapes may look wrong. If}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00136}00136 \textcolor{comment}{//   this turns out to be a problem, you can re-\/enable the old rasterizer with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00137}00137 \textcolor{comment}{//        \#define STBTT\_RASTERIZER\_VERSION 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00138}00138 \textcolor{comment}{//   which will incur about a 15\% speed hit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00139}00139 \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00149}00149 \textcolor{comment}{//      Codepoint}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00150}00150 \textcolor{comment}{//         Characters are defined by unicode codepoints, e.g. 65 is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00151}00151 \textcolor{comment}{//         uppercase A, 231 is lowercase c with a cedilla, 0x7e30 is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00152}00152 \textcolor{comment}{//         the hiragana for "{}ma"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00153}00153 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00154}00154 \textcolor{comment}{//      Glyph}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00155}00155 \textcolor{comment}{//         A visual character shape (every codepoint is rendered as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00156}00156 \textcolor{comment}{//         some glyph)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00157}00157 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00158}00158 \textcolor{comment}{//      Glyph index}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00159}00159 \textcolor{comment}{//         A font-\/specific integer ID representing a glyph}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00160}00160 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00161}00161 \textcolor{comment}{//      Baseline}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00162}00162 \textcolor{comment}{//         Glyph shapes are defined relative to a baseline, which is the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00163}00163 \textcolor{comment}{//         bottom of uppercase characters. Characters extend both above}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00164}00164 \textcolor{comment}{//         and below the baseline.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00165}00165 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00166}00166 \textcolor{comment}{//      Current Point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00167}00167 \textcolor{comment}{//         As you draw text to the screen, you keep track of a "{}current point"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00168}00168 \textcolor{comment}{//         which is the origin of each character. The current point's vertical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00169}00169 \textcolor{comment}{//         position is the baseline. Even "{}baked fonts"{} use this model.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00170}00170 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00171}00171 \textcolor{comment}{//      Vertical Font Metrics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00172}00172 \textcolor{comment}{//         The vertical qualities of the font, used to vertically position}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00173}00173 \textcolor{comment}{//         and space the characters. See docs for stbtt\_GetFontVMetrics.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00174}00174 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00175}00175 \textcolor{comment}{//      Font Size in Pixels or Points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00176}00176 \textcolor{comment}{//         The preferred interface for specifying font sizes in stb\_truetype}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00177}00177 \textcolor{comment}{//         is to specify how tall the font's vertical extent should be in pixels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00178}00178 \textcolor{comment}{//         If that sounds good enough, skip the next paragraph.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00179}00179 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00180}00180 \textcolor{comment}{//         Most font APIs instead use "{}points"{}, which are a common typographic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00181}00181 \textcolor{comment}{//         measurement for describing font size, defined as 72 points per inch.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00182}00182 \textcolor{comment}{//         stb\_truetype provides a point API for compatibility. However, true}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00183}00183 \textcolor{comment}{//         "{}per inch"{} conventions don't make much sense on computer displays}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00184}00184 \textcolor{comment}{//         since different monitors have different number of pixels per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00185}00185 \textcolor{comment}{//         inch. For example, Windows traditionally uses a convention that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00186}00186 \textcolor{comment}{//         there are 96 pixels per inch, thus making 'inch' measurements have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00187}00187 \textcolor{comment}{//         nothing to do with inches, and thus effectively defining a point to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00188}00188 \textcolor{comment}{//         be 1.333 pixels. Additionally, the TrueType font data provides}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00189}00189 \textcolor{comment}{//         an explicit scale factor to scale a given font's glyphs to points,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00190}00190 \textcolor{comment}{//         but the author has observed that this scale factor is often wrong}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00191}00191 \textcolor{comment}{//         for non-\/commercial fonts, thus making fonts scaled in points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00192}00192 \textcolor{comment}{//         according to the TrueType spec incoherently sized in practice.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00193}00193 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00194}00194 \textcolor{comment}{// DETAILED USAGE:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00195}00195 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00196}00196 \textcolor{comment}{//  Scale:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00197}00197 \textcolor{comment}{//    Select how high you want the font to be, in points or pixels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00198}00198 \textcolor{comment}{//    Call ScaleForPixelHeight or ScaleForMappingEmToPixels to compute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00199}00199 \textcolor{comment}{//    a scale factor SF that will be used by all other functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00200}00200 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00201}00201 \textcolor{comment}{//  Baseline:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00202}00202 \textcolor{comment}{//    You need to select a y-\/coordinate that is the baseline of where}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00203}00203 \textcolor{comment}{//    your text will appear. Call GetFontBoundingBox to get the baseline-\/relative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00204}00204 \textcolor{comment}{//    bounding box for all characters. SF*-\/y0 will be the distance in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00205}00205 \textcolor{comment}{//    that the worst-\/case character could extend above the baseline, so if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00206}00206 \textcolor{comment}{//    you want the top edge of characters to appear at the top of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00207}00207 \textcolor{comment}{//    screen where y=0, then you would set the baseline to SF*-\/y0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00208}00208 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00209}00209 \textcolor{comment}{//  Current point:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00210}00210 \textcolor{comment}{//    Set the current point where the first character will appear. The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00211}00211 \textcolor{comment}{//    first character could extend left of the current point; this is font}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00212}00212 \textcolor{comment}{//    dependent. You can either choose a current point that is the leftmost}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00213}00213 \textcolor{comment}{//    point and hope, or add some padding, or check the bounding box or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00214}00214 \textcolor{comment}{//    left-\/side-\/bearing of the first character to be displayed and set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00215}00215 \textcolor{comment}{//    the current point based on that.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00216}00216 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00217}00217 \textcolor{comment}{//  Displaying a character:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00218}00218 \textcolor{comment}{//    Compute the bounding box of the character. It will contain signed values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00219}00219 \textcolor{comment}{//    relative to <current\_point, baseline>. I.e. if it returns x0,y0,x1,y1,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00220}00220 \textcolor{comment}{//    then the character should be displayed in the rectangle from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00221}00221 \textcolor{comment}{//    <current\_point+SF*x0, baseline+SF*y0> to <current\_point+SF*x1,baseline+SF*y1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00222}00222 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00223}00223 \textcolor{comment}{//  Advancing for the next character:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00224}00224 \textcolor{comment}{//    Call GlyphHMetrics, and compute 'current\_point += SF * advance'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00225}00225 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00226}00226 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00227}00227 \textcolor{comment}{// ADVANCED USAGE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00228}00228 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00229}00229 \textcolor{comment}{//   Quality:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00230}00230 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00231}00231 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Use the functions with Subpixel at the end to allow your characters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00232}00232 \textcolor{comment}{//      to have subpixel positioning. Since the font is anti-\/aliased, not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00233}00233 \textcolor{comment}{//      hinted, this is very import for quality. (This is not possible with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00234}00234 \textcolor{comment}{//      baked fonts.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00235}00235 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00236}00236 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Kerning is now supported, and if you're supporting subpixel rendering}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00237}00237 \textcolor{comment}{//      then kerning is worth using to give your text a polished look.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00238}00238 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00239}00239 \textcolor{comment}{//   Performance:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00240}00240 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00241}00241 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Convert Unicode codepoints to glyph indexes and operate on the glyphs;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00242}00242 \textcolor{comment}{//      if you don't do this, stb\_truetype is forced to do the conversion on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00243}00243 \textcolor{comment}{//      every call.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00244}00244 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00245}00245 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ There are a lot of memory allocations. We should modify it to take}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00246}00246 \textcolor{comment}{//      a temp buffer and allocate from the temp buffer (without freeing),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00247}00247 \textcolor{comment}{//      should help performance a lot.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00248}00248 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00249}00249 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00250}00250 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00251}00251 \textcolor{comment}{//   The system uses the raw data found in the .ttf file without changing it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00252}00252 \textcolor{comment}{//   and without building auxiliary data structures. This is a bit inefficient}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00253}00253 \textcolor{comment}{//   on little-\/endian systems (the data is big-\/endian), but assuming you're}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00254}00254 \textcolor{comment}{//   caching the bitmaps or glyph shapes this shouldn't be a big deal.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00255}00255 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00256}00256 \textcolor{comment}{//   It appears to be very hard to programmatically determine what font a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00257}00257 \textcolor{comment}{//   given file is in a general way. I provide an API for this, but I don't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00258}00258 \textcolor{comment}{//   recommend it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00259}00259 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00260}00260 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00261}00261 \textcolor{comment}{// PERFORMANCE MEASUREMENTS FOR 1.06:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00588}00588 STBTT\_DEF \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}  stbtt\_PackBegin(\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt__pack__context}{stbtt\_pack\_context}} *spc, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *pixels, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} width, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} height, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stride\_in\_bytes, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} padding, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *alloc\_context);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00589}00589 \textcolor{comment}{// Initializes a packing context stored in the passed-\/in stbtt\_pack\_context.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00590}00590 \textcolor{comment}{// Future calls using this context will pack characters into the bitmap passed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00591}00591 \textcolor{comment}{// in here: a 1-\/channel bitmap that is width * height. stride\_in\_bytes is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00592}00592 \textcolor{comment}{// the distance from one row to the next (or 0 to mean they are packed tightly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00593}00593 \textcolor{comment}{// together). "{}padding"{} is the amount of padding to leave between each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00594}00594 \textcolor{comment}{// character (normally you want '1' for bitmaps you'll use as textures with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00595}00595 \textcolor{comment}{// bilinear filtering).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00597}00597 \textcolor{comment}{// Returns 0 on failure, 1 on success.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00606}00606 \textcolor{comment}{// Creates character bitmaps from the font\_index'th font found in fontdata (use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00607}00607 \textcolor{comment}{// font\_index=0 if you don't know what that is). It creates num\_chars\_in\_range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00608}00608 \textcolor{comment}{// bitmaps for characters with unicode values starting at first\_unicode\_char\_in\_range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00609}00609 \textcolor{comment}{// and increasing. Data for how to render them is stored in chardata\_for\_range;}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00611}00611 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00612}00612 \textcolor{comment}{// font\_size is the full height of the character from ascender to descender,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00613}00613 \textcolor{comment}{// as computed by stbtt\_ScaleForPixelHeight. To use a point size as computed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00614}00614 \textcolor{comment}{// by stbtt\_ScaleForMappingEmToPixels, wrap the point size in STBTT\_POINT\_SIZE()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00615}00615 \textcolor{comment}{// and pass that result as 'font\_size':}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00616}00616 \textcolor{comment}{//       ...,                  20 , ... // font max minus min y is 20 pixels tall}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00617}00617 \textcolor{comment}{//       ..., STBTT\_POINT\_SIZE(20), ... // 'M' is 20 pixels tall}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00618}00618 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00635}00635 STBTT\_DEF \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} stbtt\_PackSetOversampling(\mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt__pack__context}{stbtt\_pack\_context}} *spc, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} h\_oversample, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} v\_oversample);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00636}00636 \textcolor{comment}{// Oversampling a font increases the quality by allowing higher-\/quality subpixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00637}00637 \textcolor{comment}{// positioning, and is especially valuable at smaller text sizes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00638}00638 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00639}00639 \textcolor{comment}{// This function sets the amount of oversampling for all following calls to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00640}00640 \textcolor{comment}{// stbtt\_PackFontRange(s) or stbtt\_PackFontRangesGatherRects for a given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00641}00641 \textcolor{comment}{// pack context. The default (no oversampling) is achieved by h\_oversample=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00642}00642 \textcolor{comment}{// and v\_oversample=1. The total number of pixels required is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00643}00643 \textcolor{comment}{// h\_oversample*v\_oversample larger than the default; for example, 2x2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00644}00644 \textcolor{comment}{// oversampling requires 4x the storage of 1x1. For best results, render}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00645}00645 \textcolor{comment}{// oversampled textures with bilinear filtering. Look at the readme in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00646}00646 \textcolor{comment}{// stb/tests/oversample for information about oversampled fonts}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00647}00647 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00648}00648 \textcolor{comment}{// To use with PackFontRangesGather etc., you must set it before calls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00649}00649 \textcolor{comment}{// call to PackFontRangesGatherRects.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00650}00650 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00759}00759 \textcolor{comment}{// computes a scale factor to produce a font whose "{}height"{} is 'pixels' tall.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00760}00760 \textcolor{comment}{// Height is measured as the distance from the highest ascender to the lowest}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00761}00761 \textcolor{comment}{// descender; in other words, it's equivalent to calling stbtt\_GetFontVMetrics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00762}00762 \textcolor{comment}{// and computing:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00763}00763 \textcolor{comment}{//       scale = pixels / (ascent -\/ descent)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00764}00764 \textcolor{comment}{// so if you prefer to measure height by the ascent only, use a similar calculation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00765}00765 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00948}00948 STBTT\_DEF \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} * stbtt\_GetGlyphSDF(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt__fontinfo}{stbtt\_fontinfo}} *\mbox{\hyperlink{structinfo}{info}}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} scale, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} glyph, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} padding, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} onedge\_value, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} pixel\_dist\_scale, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *width, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *height, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *xoff, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *yoff);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00949}00949 STBTT\_DEF \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} * stbtt\_GetCodepointSDF(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structstbtt__fontinfo}{stbtt\_fontinfo}} *\mbox{\hyperlink{structinfo}{info}}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} scale, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} codepoint, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} padding, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} onedge\_value, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} pixel\_dist\_scale, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *width, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *height, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *xoff, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *yoff);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00950}00950 \textcolor{comment}{// These functions compute a discretized SDF field for a single character, suitable for storing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00951}00951 \textcolor{comment}{// in a single-\/channel texture, sampling with bilinear filtering, and testing against}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00952}00952 \textcolor{comment}{// larger than some threshold to produce scalable fonts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00953}00953 \textcolor{comment}{//        info              -\/-\/  the font}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00954}00954 \textcolor{comment}{//        scale             -\/-\/  controls the size of the resulting SDF bitmap, same as it would be creating a regular bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00955}00955 \textcolor{comment}{//        glyph/codepoint   -\/-\/  the character to generate the SDF for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00956}00956 \textcolor{comment}{//        padding           -\/-\/  extra "{}pixels"{} around the character which are filled with the distance to the character (not 0),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00957}00957 \textcolor{comment}{//                                 which allows effects like bit outlines}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00958}00958 \textcolor{comment}{//        onedge\_value      -\/-\/  value 0-\/255 to test the SDF against to reconstruct the character (i.e. the isocontour of the character)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00959}00959 \textcolor{comment}{//        pixel\_dist\_scale  -\/-\/  what value the SDF should increase by when moving one SDF "{}pixel"{} away from the edge (on the 0..255 scale)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00960}00960 \textcolor{comment}{//                                 if positive, > onedge\_value is inside; if negative, < onedge\_value is inside}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00961}00961 \textcolor{comment}{//        width,height      -\/-\/  output height \& width of the SDF bitmap (including padding)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00962}00962 \textcolor{comment}{//        xoff,yoff         -\/-\/  output origin of the character}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00963}00963 \textcolor{comment}{//        return value      -\/-\/  a 2D array of bytes 0..255, width*height in size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00964}00964 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00965}00965 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel\_dist\_scale \& onedge\_value are a scale \& bias that allows you to make}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00966}00966 \textcolor{comment}{// optimal use of the limited 0..255 for your application, trading off precision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00967}00967 \textcolor{comment}{// and special effects. SDF values outside the range 0..255 are clamped to 0..255.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00968}00968 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00969}00969 \textcolor{comment}{// Example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00970}00970 \textcolor{comment}{//      scale = stbtt\_ScaleForPixelHeight(22)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00971}00971 \textcolor{comment}{//      padding = 5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00972}00972 \textcolor{comment}{//      onedge\_value = 180}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00973}00973 \textcolor{comment}{//      pixel\_dist\_scale = 180/5.0 = 36.0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00974}00974 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00975}00975 \textcolor{comment}{//      This will create an SDF bitmap in which the character is about 22 pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00976}00976 \textcolor{comment}{//      high but the whole bitmap is about 22+5+5=32 pixels high. To produce a filled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00977}00977 \textcolor{comment}{//      shape, sample the SDF at each pixel and fill the pixel if the SDF value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00978}00978 \textcolor{comment}{//      is greater than or equal to 180/255. (You'll actually want to antialias,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00979}00979 \textcolor{comment}{//      which is beyond the scope of this example.) Additionally, you can compute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00980}00980 \textcolor{comment}{//      offset outlines (e.g. to stroke the character border inside \& outside,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00981}00981 \textcolor{comment}{//      or only outside). For example, to fill outside the character up to 3 SDF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00982}00982 \textcolor{comment}{//      pixels, you would compare against (180-\/36.0*3)/255 = 72/255. The above}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00983}00983 \textcolor{comment}{//      choice of variables maps a range from 5 pixels outside the shape to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00984}00984 \textcolor{comment}{//      2 pixels inside the shape to 0..255; this is intended primarily for apply}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00985}00985 \textcolor{comment}{//      outside effects only (the interior range is needed to allow proper}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00986}00986 \textcolor{comment}{//      antialiasing of the font at *smaller* sizes)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00987}00987 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00988}00988 \textcolor{comment}{// The function computes the SDF analytically at each SDF pixel, not by e.g.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00989}00989 \textcolor{comment}{// building a higher-\/res bitmap and approximating it. In theory the quality}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00990}00990 \textcolor{comment}{// should be as high as possible for an SDF of this size \& representation, but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00991}00991 \textcolor{comment}{// unclear if this is true in practice (perhaps building a higher-\/res bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00992}00992 \textcolor{comment}{// and computing from that can allow drop-\/out prevention).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00993}00993 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00994}00994 \textcolor{comment}{// The algorithm has not been optimized at all, so expect it to be slow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00995}00995 \textcolor{comment}{// if computing lots of characters or very large sizes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00996}00996 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l00997}00997 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01002}01002 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01003}01003 \textcolor{comment}{// You should really just solve this offline, keep your own tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01004}01004 \textcolor{comment}{// of what font is what, and don't try to get it out of the .ttf file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01005}01005 \textcolor{comment}{// That's because getting it out of the .ttf file is really hard, because}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01006}01006 \textcolor{comment}{// the names in the file can appear in many possible encodings, in many}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01007}01007 \textcolor{comment}{// possible languages, and e.g. if you need a case-\/insensitive comparison,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01008}01008 \textcolor{comment}{// the details of that depend on the encoding \& language in a complex way}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01009}01009 \textcolor{comment}{// (actually underspecified in truetype, but also gigantic).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01010}01010 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01011}01011 \textcolor{comment}{// But you can use the provided functions in two possible ways:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01012}01012 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbtt\_FindMatchingFont() will use *case-\/sensitive* comparisons on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01013}01013 \textcolor{comment}{//             unicode-\/encoded names to try to find the font you want;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01014}01014 \textcolor{comment}{//             you can run this before calling stbtt\_InitFont()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01015}01015 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01016}01016 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbtt\_GetFontNameString() lets you get any of the various strings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01017}01017 \textcolor{comment}{//             from the file yourself and do your own comparisons on them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01018}01018 \textcolor{comment}{//             You have to have called stbtt\_InitFont() first.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01019}01019 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01776}01776                scy = y;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01784}01784                   sy = (stbtt\_int32) vertices[off+i+1].y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01785}01785                   ++i; \textcolor{comment}{// we're using point i+1 as the starting point, so skip it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l01786}01786                \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03180}03180                \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03181}03181                \textcolor{comment}{// goal is to measure the area covered by '.' in each pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03182}03182 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03183}03183                \textcolor{comment}{// if x2 is right at the right edge of x1, y\_crossing can blow up, github \#1057}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03184}03184                \textcolor{comment}{// @TODO: maybe test against sy1 rather than y\_bottom?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03185}03185                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (y\_crossing > y\_bottom)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03186}03186                   y\_crossing = y\_bottom;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03187}03187 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03188}03188                \mbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gaf749e7f029eb88580a45493e41002629}{sign}} = \mbox{\hyperlink{group__gtc__constants_ga4b7956eb6e2fbedfc7cf2e46e85c5139}{e}}-\/>direction;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03189}03189 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03190}03190                \textcolor{comment}{// area of the rectangle covered from sy0..y\_crossing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03191}03191                area = \mbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gaf749e7f029eb88580a45493e41002629}{sign}} * (y\_crossing-\/sy0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03192}03192 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03193}03193                \textcolor{comment}{// area of the triangle (x\_top,sy0), (x1+1,sy0), (x1+1,y\_crossing)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03194}03194                scanline[x1] += stbtt\_\_sized\_triangle\_area(area, x1+1 -\/ x\_top);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03195}03195 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03196}03196                \textcolor{comment}{// check if final y\_crossing is blown up; no test case for this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03197}03197                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (y\_final > y\_bottom) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03198}03198                   y\_final = y\_bottom;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03199}03199                   dy = (y\_final -\/ y\_crossing ) / (x2 -\/ (x1+1)); \textcolor{comment}{// if denom=0, y\_final = y\_crossing, so y\_final <= y\_bottom}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03200}03200                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03201}03201 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03202}03202                \textcolor{comment}{// in second pixel, area covered by line segment found in first pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03203}03203                \textcolor{comment}{// is always a rectangle 1 wide * the height of that line segment; this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03204}03204                \textcolor{comment}{// is exactly what the variable 'area' stores. it also gets a contribution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03205}03205                \textcolor{comment}{// from the line segment within it. the THIRD pixel will get the first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03206}03206                \textcolor{comment}{// pixel's rectangle contribution, the second pixel's rectangle contribution,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03207}03207                \textcolor{comment}{// and its own contribution. the 'own contribution' is the same in every pixel except}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03208}03208                \textcolor{comment}{// the leftmost and rightmost, a trapezoid that slides down in each pixel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03209}03209                \textcolor{comment}{// the second pixel's contribution to the third pixel will be the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03210}03210                \textcolor{comment}{// rectangle 1 wide times the height change in the second pixel, which is dy.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03211}03211 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03212}03212                \mbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga015a1261ff23e12650211aa872863cce}{step}} = \mbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gaf749e7f029eb88580a45493e41002629}{sign}} * dy * 1; \textcolor{comment}{// dy is dy/dx, change in y for every 1 change in x,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03213}03213                \textcolor{comment}{// which multiplied by 1-\/pixel-\/width is how much pixel area changes for each step in x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03214}03214                \textcolor{comment}{// so the area advances by 'step' every time}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03215}03215 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03216}03216                \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (x = x1+1; x < x2; ++x) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03217}03217                   scanline[x] += area + \mbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga015a1261ff23e12650211aa872863cce}{step}}/2; \textcolor{comment}{// area of trapezoid is 1*step/2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03218}03218                   area += \mbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_ga015a1261ff23e12650211aa872863cce}{step}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03219}03219                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03220}03220                STBTT\_assert(STBTT\_fabs(area) <= 1.01f); \textcolor{comment}{// accumulated error from area += step unless we round step down}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03221}03221                STBTT\_assert(sy1 > y\_final-\/0.01f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03222}03222 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03223}03223                \textcolor{comment}{// area covered in the last pixel is the rectangle from all the pixels to the left,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03224}03224                \textcolor{comment}{// plus the trapezoid filled by the line segment in this pixel all the way to the right edge}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03225}03225                scanline[x2] += area + \mbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gaf749e7f029eb88580a45493e41002629}{sign}} * stbtt\_\_position\_trapezoid\_area(sy1-\/y\_final, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}) x2, x2+1.0f, x\_bottom, x2+1.0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03226}03226 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03227}03227                \textcolor{comment}{// the rest of the line is filled based on the total height of the line segment in this pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03228}03228                scanline\_fill[x2] += \mbox{\hyperlink{group__core__func__common_gaf749e7f029eb88580a45493e41002629}{sign}} * (sy1-\/sy0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03229}03229             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03230}03230          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03231}03231             \textcolor{comment}{// if edge goes outside of box we're drawing, we require}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03232}03232             \textcolor{comment}{// clipping logic. since this does not match the intended use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03233}03233             \textcolor{comment}{// of this library, we use a different, very slow brute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03234}03234             \textcolor{comment}{// force implementation}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03238}03238             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03239}03239             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (x=0; x < len; ++x) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03240}03240                \textcolor{comment}{// cases:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03241}03241                \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03242}03242                \textcolor{comment}{// there can be up to two intersections with the pixel. any intersection}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03243}03243                \textcolor{comment}{// with left or right edges can be handled by splitting into two (or three)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03244}03244                \textcolor{comment}{// regions. intersections with top \& bottom do not necessitate case-\/wise logic.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03245}03245                \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03246}03246                \textcolor{comment}{// the old way of doing this found the intersections with the left \& right edges,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03247}03247                \textcolor{comment}{// then used some simple logic to produce up to three segments in sorted order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03248}03248                \textcolor{comment}{// from top-\/to-\/bottom. however, this had a problem: if an x edge was epsilon}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03249}03249                \textcolor{comment}{// across the x border, then the corresponding y position might not be distinct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03250}03250                \textcolor{comment}{// from the other y segment, and it might ignored as an empty segment. to avoid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03251}03251                \textcolor{comment}{// that, we need to explicitly produce segments based on x positions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03252}03252 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03253}03253                \textcolor{comment}{// rename variables to clearly-\/defined pairs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03254}03254                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y0 = y\_top;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03255}03255                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} x1 = (float) (x);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03256}03256                \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} x2 = (float) (x+1);}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03259}03259 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l03260}03260                \textcolor{comment}{// x = e-\/>x + e-\/>dx * (y-\/y\_top)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04115}04115             \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04141}04141    \textcolor{comment}{// The prefilter is a box filter of width "{}oversample"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04142}04142    \textcolor{comment}{// which shifts phase by (oversample -\/ 1)/2 pixels in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04143}04143    \textcolor{comment}{// oversampled space. We want to shift in the opposite}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04144}04144    \textcolor{comment}{// direction to counter this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04145}04145    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{float})-\/(oversample -\/ 1) / (2.0f * (\textcolor{keywordtype}{float})oversample);}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04398}04398 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbtt\_\_ray\_intersect\_bezier(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float} orig[2], \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ray[2], \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} q0[2], \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} q1[2], \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} q2[2], \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} hits[2][2])}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04400}04400    \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} q0perp = q0[1]*ray[0] -\/ q0[0]*ray[1];}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04405}04405    \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = q0perp -\/ 2*q1perp + q2perp;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04407}04407    \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} c = q0perp -\/ roperp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04408}04408 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04409}04409    \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} s0 = 0., s1 = 0.;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04410}04410    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} num\_s = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04411}04411 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04412}04412    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (a != 0.0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04413}04413       \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} discr = b*b -\/ a*c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04414}04414       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (discr > 0.0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04415}04415          \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} rcpna = -\/1 / a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04416}04416          \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} d = (float) STBTT\_sqrt(discr);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04417}04417          s0 = (b+d) * rcpna;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04418}04418          s1 = (b-\/d) * rcpna;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04419}04419          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (s0 >= 0.0 \&\& s0 <= 1.0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04420}04420             num\_s = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04421}04421          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (d > 0.0 \&\& s1 >= 0.0 \&\& s1 <= 1.0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04422}04422             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (num\_s == 0) s0 = s1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04423}04423             ++num\_s;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04424}04424          \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04426}04426    \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04427}04427       \textcolor{comment}{// 2*b*s + c = 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04428}04428       \textcolor{comment}{// s = -\/c / (2*b)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04544}04544 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} stbtt\_\_solve\_cubic(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} b, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} c, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}* r)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04691}04691                         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} c = mx*ax+my*ay;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04692}04692                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (a == 0.0) \{ \textcolor{comment}{// if a is 0, it's linear}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04703}04703                               res[1] = (-\/b + root)/(2*a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__truetype_8h_source_l04704}04704                               num = 2; \textcolor{comment}{// don't bother distinguishing 1-\/solution case, as code below will still work}}
